# Changelog — The Endless Staircase

All notable changes to the playable game. Newest first. Built from Toby's
"Secret of Simon's Lore" emails (Lore 25). Live game:
https://d1hysvqh647i13.cloudfront.net/game/endless-staircase/

## 2026-07-23 — SHARES FIRST WITH PERO (BEAT 164)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-23 lore (forty-ninth message of the "More Classics Era" thread, sent seventeen minutes after THE VILLAIN OF THE GAME and raising Luigi Green from second main character to equal-top with the creator).

Toby's words, and this is the whole of what he wrote himself: *"Pero goes easy on you since he is the creator, and Luigi Green never goes easy and is DETERMIND to destroy everyone and everything. Luigi Green absorbed Mr. Black and Gray, Simon 404 is hanged on a green orb floating above Luigi Green's hand. Luigi Green can CONTROL Classics unlike all other characters. Pero is the creator of Classics and can control it, he can control any character, Pero isn't included in 'everyone' because he created everyone. Luigi Green now turns the rest into minor villians (Pero/Tunner still is a major villian, only Pero/Tunner and Luigi Green are real villians), Luigi Green can just destroy all below him (Luigi Green and Pero are now at the same power level), Luigi Green takes every spot and Pero shares 1st with him."* (Everything after that paragraph is a pasted ChatGPT recap — the equal-top framing, the two-villain list, the difference table, the absorbed-power breakdown, and the "clean canon update." It is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own paragraph.)

- New BEAT 164 lore panel, SHARES FIRST WITH PERO, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3326,3348)`, cycle length extended `3326 → 3348`). `LV_BEATS` now 165 entries (0-164). He leaves the seats under Pero (BEAT 162) and joins Pero at the top.
- **THE WHOLE LINE box, left column** — Toby's line on its own, above the header *THE CREATOR GOES EASY. HE DOES NOT.* Behind everything, a green-and-gold ladder of rungs, the two colors sharing the light.
- **HE NEVER GOES EASY panel** (center) — *DETERMINED TO DESTROY EVERYONE AND EVERYTHING.* The `drawLuigiGreen` figure holds **Simon 404** captured in a **green orb** floating above his hand (a red blob with a jagged look, hung on a line off his hand), while **Mr. Black** (dark) and **Gray** (grey) motes are pulled in and absorbed into him. Caption: *he absorbed Mr. Black and Gray, and hangs Simon 404 in a green orb over his hand.*
- **THE TOP IS SHARED panel** (right) — *SAME POWER LEVEL, HE TAKES EVERY SPOT.* One seat **1** split down the middle, gold on the left and green on the right: **PERO / TUNNER** *(GOES EASY)* and **LUIGI GREEN** *(NEVER DOES)* sharing it. Under the seat, **EVERYONE ELSE · MINOR VILLAINS**.
- **ONLY TWO REAL VILLAINS box** (left, under the beat ladder) — **★ MAJOR — PERO / TUNNER** and **★ MAJOR — LUIGI GREEN** above a rule, then **· MINOR — EVERYONE ELSE** *(New Chara, Simon 404, Oren, all of them, minor villains under him now, any of them destroyable at will)*.
- **WHAT MAKES THEM EQUAL panel** (right, lower) — *BOTH CAN CONTROL CLASSICS.* Characters can gain power, corrupt the game, consume realms; only Pero could control Classics itself, and now Luigi Green can too, which is why he shares first. The temperament split: **PERO** *(controls everyone but goes easy, and is not part of "everyone" because he made the game)* vs **LUIGI GREEN** *(controls Classics too, and uses it at full force on everyone under him)*.
- Closing lines in the middle column: *THE CREATOR HAS A SEATMATE NOW.* then *AND THE SEATMATE NEVER GOES EASY.*
- Insight banner: *"LUIGI GREEN ABSORBED MR. BLACK AND GRAY, CAGED SIMON 404, CAN CONTROL CLASSICS, AND NOW SHARES FIRST WITH PERO,"* and the star banner *"★ TWO REAL VILLAINS LEFT — PERO/TUNNER AND LUIGI GREEN — SHARING FIRST · EVERYONE ELSE IS MINOR ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `sharesfirst` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

![Shares First With Pero](screenshots/226-shares-first-with-pero.png)

## 2026-07-23 — THE VILLAIN OF THE GAME (BEAT 163)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-23 lore (forty-eighth message of the "More Classics Era" thread, a reply in the "Even more Classics Era" thread, sent four minutes after LUIGI GREEN and turning the character it just built).

Toby's words, and this is the whole of what he wrote himself: *"Luigi Green is litterly the villian of the game, he also steals everyone's power and uses all the power to make him loved by Pero and to destroy everyone else."* (Everything after that line in the email is a pasted ChatGPT recap — the "fake-beloved villain," the "favor power" reading, the numbered villain structure, the "clean canon update," and a full quote of the previous email. It is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own line.)

- New BEAT 163 lore panel, THE VILLAIN OF THE GAME, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3304,3326)`, cycle length extended `3304 → 3326`). `LV_BEATS` now 164 entries (0-163). Directly turns BEAT 162: the good-guy look was a disguise.
- **THE WHOLE LINE box, left column** — Toby's sentence on its own, above the header *THE GOOD-GUY LOOK WAS THE DISGUISE. HE IS THE VILLAIN.* Behind everything, the green ladder of rungs from BEAT 162 now bleeds red where his theft touches it.
- **THE VILLAIN OF THE GAME panel** (center) — *HE STEALS EVERYONE'S POWER AND KEEPS IT.* Nine cast source-dots sit on a ring and drain grey as red power streams pulse inward into Luigi Green at the center; a red villain aura swells behind the `drawLuigiGreen` figure and his eyes glint red. Caption: *the good-guy look from BEAT 162 was the disguise, every power he has came off somebody else.*
- **HE DOES NOT TRAIN. HE TAKES. box** (left, under the beat ladder) — **STEALS EVERYONE'S POWER** *(not combat he earned, power he took off the whole cast)* ▸ **SPENT ON BEING LOVED** *(goal 1: use the stolen power to make Pero favor him)* ▸ **SPENT ON DESTROYING** *(goal 2: use the same stolen power to destroy everyone else)* ▸ **ABOVE MR. BLACK NOW** *(he takes the main-villain spot Mr. Black used to hold)*.
- **WHAT HE SPENDS IT ON panel** (right) — *TWO GOALS, IN TOBY'S OWN WORDS*: **1 MAKE PERO LOVE HIM** in violet *(the stolen power buys the creator's favor; Pero's "I won't let you touch him" from BEAT 162 is the theft working, not a coincidence)* and **2 DESTROY EVERYONE ELSE** in red *(the same stolen power, turned outward on the cast he took it from)*.
- **WHY HE IS ALMOST IMPOSSIBLE box** (right, under the panel) — fighting him is not fighting one character, it is fighting all three at once: **LUIGI GREEN** *(green)* **+ STOLEN POWER** *(orange)* **+ PERO'S FAVORITISM** *(violet)*.
- Closing lines in the middle column: *HIS POWER IS NOT ONLY FOR FIGHTING. IT IS FOR BEING LOVED.* then *AND PERO STILL WON'T LET ANYONE TOUCH HIM.*
- Insight banner: *"LUIGI GREEN STEALS EVERYONE'S POWER AND SPENDS IT ON BEING LOVED BY PERO AND DESTROYING EVERYONE ELSE,"* and the star banner *"★ THE VILLAIN OF THE GAME · HE STEALS POWER · GOAL 1: PERO'S LOVE · GOAL 2: DESTROY EVERYONE ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `villain` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

![The Villain of the Game](screenshots/225-villain-of-the-game.png)

## 2026-07-23 — LUIGI GREEN (BEAT 162)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-23 lore (forty-seventh message of the "More Classics Era" thread, subject "Even more Classics Era," and the eighth of July 23, sent about half an hour after NO SECOND PLACE and reopening the seat that beat had just closed).

Toby's words, and this is the whole of his own opening paragraph: *"Luigi Green now takes New Chara's spot, New Chara is now fourth in power, Luigi Green takes second and third. Luigi Green now has forms that take all New Chara's spots on the power level, Luigi Green takes all the spots from second to infinitith, and Pero/Tunner takes first. Luigi Green uses a bunch of Au Green, Green Orbs, Cat Power from Simon 404, Anti Virus from Simon 404, and is Simon 404's main rival/enemy, and is a game consumer. Luigi Green is the second main character and always battles with Simon 404. Luigi Green now won. He looks like a good guy, but he is not Luigi Mario, he is Luigi Green, a whole different person, like the one who is the current most well known Classics character, he is rivals with everyone and wins. Pero seems to love Luigi Green over everyone else, and when I asked, he said 'This is the best character in the game, I won't let you touch him!'"* (Everything after that paragraph in the email is a pasted ChatGPT recap — the "Luigi Green power takeover," the numbered board, the powers list and the "clean canon update." It is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own paragraph.)

- New BEAT 162 lore panel, LUIGI GREEN, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3282,3304)`, cycle length extended `3282 → 3304`). `LV_BEATS` now 163 entries (0-162). A returning character: Luigi Green already had a crystal reserve (BEAT 8), won the domain clash (BEAT 9), and has a green cat-power form drawn by the existing `drawLuigiGreen` — this beat raises him to the #2 seat and reuses that same figure.
- **THE WHOLE LINE box, left column** — Toby's opening sentences on their own, above the header *THE CLOSED SEAT DID NOT STAY CLOSED. SOMEBODY GREEN WALKED INTO IT.* Behind everything, a green ladder of rungs climbs upward, filling the whole board.
- **THE BOARD NOW panel** (center) — *ONE SEAT ON TOP, ONE NAME ON EVERYTHING BELOW IT.* **1 PERO** *and* **TUNNER** keep the shared gold top seat from BEAT 161 *(he did not touch the top)* ▸ **2 → ∞ LUIGI GREEN** in green, a tall box with a ghosted stack of rungs inside *(he took second and third, and his forms fill every seat from second to infinitith — the seat BEAT 161 closed, reopened and stacked all the way down)* ▸ **4 NEW CHARA** in white *(third an hour ago, fourth now; his forms took the seats above her, she lost no fight, the ladder just grew over her)*.
- **WHAT HE BRINGS box** (left, under the beat ladder) — he is not new power, he took it off the board and off Simon 404 and turns it on Simon 404: **AU GREEN** *(his own green AU)* ▸ **GREEN ORBS** *(the orb tools in green; his BEAT 8 crystal reserve)* ▸ **CAT POWER** *(taken from Simon 404, the same power his form already wears)* ▸ **ANTI-VIRUS** *(also taken from Simon 404, so he fights Simon with Simon's own cure)* ▸ **A GAME CONSUMER** *(he can consume the game itself, the power that puts him above everyone under Pero)*.
- **THE SECOND MAIN CHARACTER panel** (right) — *NOT LUIGI MARIO — A WHOLE DIFFERENT PERSON.* The Luigi Green figure is drawn by `drawLuigiGreen` with his cat-power aura rising, over **SIMON 404'S MAIN RIVAL / ENEMY** *(he always battles Simon 404, and uses Simon's own Cat Power and Anti-Virus to do it)*, **LUIGI GREEN NOW WON** and *RIVALS WITH EVERYONE, AND WINS.*
- **PERO'S FAVORITE box** (right, under the panel) — Pero never liked anyone winning his game; this time he loves the winner over everyone else, and he said: *"THIS IS THE BEST CHARACTER IN THE GAME, I WON'T LET YOU TOUCH HIM!"*
- Closing lines in the middle column: *HE TOOK SECOND, THIRD, AND EVERY SEAT DOWN TO INFINITY.* then *AND PERO WON'T LET ANYONE TOUCH HIM.*
- Insight banner: *"LUIGI GREEN TAKES EVERY SEAT FROM SECOND TO INFINITITH — NEW CHARA DROPS TO FOURTH, PERO/TUNNER STAYS FIRST,"* and the star banner *"★ THE SECOND MAIN CHARACTER · SIMON 404'S RIVAL · A GAME CONSUMER · PERO'S FAVORITE ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `luigigreen` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

![Luigi Green](screenshots/224-luigi-green.png)

## 2026-07-23 — NO SECOND PLACE (BEAT 161)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-23 lore (forty-sixth message of the "More Classics Era" thread, and the seventh of July 23, sent an hour and twenty minutes after THE THIRD STRONGEST and answering the question that beat left open: does the board count bodies or beings?).

Toby's words, and this is the whole of what he wrote himself: *"The power level is 1. Pero and Tunner (no 2 since there are two beings shared as 1), 3. New Chara."* (Everything after that line in the email is a pasted ChatGPT recap — the "no #2" explanation, the creator/vessel role split, the list of what New Chara still carries, and the "clean canon update" restatement. It is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own line.)

- New BEAT 161 lore panel, NO SECOND PLACE, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3260,3282)`, cycle length extended `3260 → 3282`). `LV_BEATS` now 162 entries (0-161).
- **THE WHOLE LINE box, left column** — Toby's one sentence on its own, above the header *THE SEAT ABOVE HER WAS NOT GIVEN AWAY. IT WAS CLOSED.* Behind everything, the same drifting ladder of rungs as BEAT 160, except one rung in the middle is missing all the way across.
- **THE BOARD NOW panel** (center) — *TWO SEATS FILLED, AND A NUMBER THAT IS GONE.* **1 PERO** *and* **TUNNER** share a single gold box *(two beings shared as 1; they do not stack up the board any more, they sit in one seat together)* ▸ slot **2** is drawn as a hole: a dashed grey outline reading **THERE IS NO 2** *(the seat was not lost and it was not won, it was folded into the one above it)*, with a gold line struck through it ▸ **3 NEW CHARA** in white *(same number as an hour ago, with one fewer being above her; LV, KR, the Dreemurr powers and the swords are all still on her)*.
- **IT COUNTS BEINGS, NOT BODIES box** (left, under the beat ladder) — the rule that settles what BEAT 160 left open: **ONE BEING, ONE SEAT** *(Pero and Tunner share the top, they are not 1 and 2 any more)* ▸ **A NAME BUYS NOTHING** *(BEAT 158 gave him a second body; it does not get its own place on the board)* ▸ **THE 2 IS TAKEN AWAY** *(not handed down; the number is retired with the seat it belonged to)* ▸ **SHE STAYS AT 3** *(nobody is promoted into a seat nobody lost a fight for)* ▸ **THE GAP STAYS OPEN** *(there is a hole in the middle of the board and it is supposed to be there)*.
- **SECOND BEING, THIRD NUMBER panel** (right) — *THE COUNT AND THE RANK STOPPED AGREEING*, lighting up one at a time: **2** *(beings on the whole board — Pero and Tunner are one of them, New Chara is the other)* ▸ **2ND** *(where she actually stands: one being is above her, so she is the second strongest thing in the game)* ▸ **3RD** *(what she is still called: Toby wrote 3, not 2, and the number stayed where it was when she had two above her)*.
- **WHAT THE RULE SHUTS box** (under the right panel) — **HE CANNOT COLLECT SEATS WITH NAMES** *(a third name or a fourth would fold into the same seat now, instead of pushing everyone else further down)* / **AND NOBODY CLIMBS INTO A CLOSED SEAT** *(the 2 went away with the merge; it is not sitting there waiting for the next character to win it)*.
- Closing lines in the middle column: *THE TWO NAMES BECAME ONE SEAT.* then *AND SHE DID NOT MOVE UP INTO THE SPACE.*
- Insight banner: *"THE BOARD COUNTS BEINGS — SHE IS THE SECOND BEING ON IT AND SHE IS STILL CALLED THE THIRD,"* and the star banner *"★ 1. PERO AND TUNNER · NO 2, SINCE THERE ARE TWO BEINGS SHARED AS 1 · 3. NEW CHARA ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `nosecondplace` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

![No Second Place](screenshots/223-no-second-place.png)

## 2026-07-23 — THE THIRD STRONGEST (BEAT 160)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-23 lore (forty-fifth message of the "More Classics Era" thread, and the sixth of July 23, sent just under an hour after HE WASN'T JOKING).

Toby's words, and this is the whole of what he wrote himself: *"New Chara became the third strongest (under Tunner and Pero)."* (Everything after that line in the email is a pasted ChatGPT recap — the numbered 1 Pero / 2 Tunner / 3 New Chara board with its explanations, the bullet list of what Tunner secretly does, the list of what New Chara still has, and the "clean canon update" paragraph. It is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own line. The recap does restate things already on file from BEATS 157-159.)

- New BEAT 160 lore panel, THE THIRD STRONGEST, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3238,3260)`, cycle length extended `3238 → 3260`). `LV_BEATS` now 161 entries (0-160).
- **THE WHOLE LINE box, left column** — Toby's one sentence on its own, above the header *SHE DID NOT MOVE. THE NAMES ABOVE HER DID.* Behind everything, a slow ladder of rungs drifts upward, because the board keeps rearranging.
- **THE TOP THREE panel** (center) — *THREE SEATS, AND ONLY TWO BEINGS SITTING IN THEM.* **1 PERO** in gold *(still the highest; he made the game, the systems, the realms and the rules)* ▸ **2 TUNNER** in violet *(secretly Pero's Phase 2 vessel, sitting in a normal Phase 1 slot, BEAT 157)* ▸ **3 NEW CHARA** in white *(LV, KR, the Dreemurr powers and the swords — and the highest seat that is somebody else)*.
- **The bracket.** A violet bracket is drawn down the left edge of slots 1 and 2, joining them, with the **ONE AND TWO ARE THE SAME BEING** box under the board: *BEAT 158 — 2 bodies with different names, but in Sprunki they are considered the same being. So the highest seat held by anybody else is the third one.*
- **NOTHING WAS TAKEN OFF HER box** (left, under the beat ladder) — her seat moved and she did not lose one thing she owns, and all of it is already on file from earlier beats: **LV** *(mined one fight at a time, smallest AUs upward, BEAT 131)* ▸ **KR** *(she revives with it, so losing is not the end of her)* ▸ **ALL THE DREEMURR POWERS** *(handed over whole, not won piece by piece)* ▸ **THE DREEMURR TOOLS & SWORDS** *(the Asriel Sword, the Hyperdeath Syche, and anything she needs)* ▸ **HER CUTSCENE BATTLE STYLE** *(Toby called hers the most intense battle in the mod)* ▸ **THE CLASSICS DEMON IDENTITY** *(the white cloak, all her cloaths white)*.
- **WHERE HER SEAT HAS BEEN panel** (right) — *THREE DIFFERENT SEATS IN UNDER A DAY*, lighting up one at a time: **2ND** *(Jul 22, 4:02 PM — ALL OF THE DREEMURR POWERS, the whole Dreemurr side arrived at once)* ▸ **4TH** *(Jul 23, 6:43 AM — NOT ALL AT ONCE, Simon 404 came back to second and she slid to fourth with Oren and others)* ▸ **3RD** *(Jul 23, 11:29 AM — now, under Tunner and Pero, and she never fought either of them for it)*.
- **AND LOOK WHO IS GONE box** (under the right panel) — **SIMON 404 WAS SECOND THIS MORNING** *(BEAT 154 put him back at second at 6:43 AM; five hours later he is not in the top three at all)* / **AND HE PAID FOR THE SEAT THAT TOOK HIS** *(BEAT 158 — the emeralds that keep Tunner out of Phase 1 come from Simon 404, five at a time, for horseshoes)*.
- Closing lines in the middle column: *SHE IS THIRD BEHIND TWO NAMES.* then *AND THE TWO NAMES ARE ONE BEING.*
- Insight banner: *"1 PERO · 2 TUNNER · 3 NEW CHARA — SHE KEPT EVERY POWER SHE HAD, AND HER SEAT MOVED ANYWAY,"* and the star banner *"★ NEW CHARA BECAME THE THIRD STRONGEST — UNDER TUNNER AND PERO ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `thirdstrongest` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

![The Third Strongest](screenshots/222-third-strongest.png)

## 2026-07-23 — HE WASN'T JOKING (BEAT 159)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-23 lore (forty-fourth message of the "More Classics Era" thread, and the fifth of July 23, sent about an hour after TWO SOULS, ONE VESSEL and going back to something Pero said a long time before any of this).

Toby's words: *"When Pero says that everyone's souls will now be his, he wasn't joking, he became Tunner and secretly Phase 2, it consumes the souls of victums, it also stalks and vanishes through the walls, it also makes the game maze scarier, and it also makes static portals to vanish and teleport, Tunner acts normal Phase 1 because Pero is smart. Pero is the best at the game, he created it."* (The pasted ChatGPT breakdown — the "hidden impostor of the maze" framing and the bullet list of everything Pero supposedly knows: every maze path, hiding spot, character weakness, portal location, ending trigger and phase rule — is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

- New BEAT 159 lore panel, HE WASN'T JOKING, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3216,3238)`, cycle length extended `3216 → 3238`). `LV_BEATS` now 160 entries (0-159).
- **The two canon lines, left column.** **THE WARNING** in blue: *"Everyone's souls will now be his"* ▸ **HE WASN'T JOKING** in violet: *"He became Tunner and secretly Phase 2."* Behind them, bands of static drift down the panel and a single shadow crosses the whole thing edge to edge without stopping at anything.
- **WHAT THE VESSEL ACTUALLY DOES box** (left, under the beat ladder) — **IT CONSUMES THE SOULS OF VICTUMS** *(not a fight move; the thing the warning promised, running quietly in the background)* ▸ **IT STALKS** *(it picks something and follows it instead of charging at it)* ▸ **IT VANISHES THROUGH THE WALLS** *(the maze does not hold him the way it holds everyone else)* ▸ **★ IT MAKES STATIC PORTALS** *(to vanish and teleport, so he leaves before anyone gets to him)*. Four powers, and not one of them is a hit.
- **HE IS COLLECTING THEM panel** (center) — *2 SOULS FOR 1 VESSEL WAS A COUNT, AND A COUNT CAN CLIMB*, with soul pips on each row: **PERO SAID IT OUT LOUD** *(1 pip; he said it in front of the cast and nobody took it literally)* ▸ **THE VESSEL EATS** *(2 pips; every soul it takes is one more holding the disguise up)* ▸ **★ SO THE COUNT GOES UP** *(3 pips, and the third one is drawn open on purpose, because BEAT 158 caught him at 2 and that was where he started, not where he stops)*.
- **The maze box** (under the center panel) — **THE MAZE ITSELF IS ONE OF HIS POWERS**: *it also makes the game maze scarier, so the room you are standing in is part of what he does to you.*
- **STATIC PORTALS panel** (right) — a drawn 6×4 maze with two static portals flickering in place and a violet figure walking straight through every wall on its way across, fading out as it reaches the far portal. *HE STALKS, HE GOES THROUGH THE WALL, HE TELEPORTS OUT.*
- **WHY HE STILL LOOKS NORMAL box** (under the right panel) — **WHAT THE BOARD SEES** *(Tunner acts normal Phase 1, because Pero is smart; none of the four powers show on the outside)* / **WHY THAT IS ENOUGH** *(Pero is the best at the game, he created it, so he does not have to look scary to be the worst thing in the maze)*.
- Closing lines in the middle column: *IT WAS NEVER A THREAT.* then *IT WAS A DESCRIPTION OF THE PLAN.*
- Insight banner: *"IT CONSUMES SOULS, STALKS, VANISHES THROUGH THE WALLS AND MAKES STATIC PORTALS TO TELEPORT — AND IT STILL READS AS PHASE 1,"* and the star banner *"★ HE WASN'T JOKING — HE BECAME TUNNER AND SECRETLY PHASE 2 ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `soulwarning` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

![He Wasn't Joking](screenshots/221-he-wasnt-joking.png)

## 2026-07-23 — TWO SOULS, ONE VESSEL (BEAT 158)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-23 lore (forty-third message of the "More Classics Era" thread, and the fourth of July 23, sent forty-seven minutes after TUNNER IS PERO and answering the thing that beat left open: how the disguise holds).

Toby's words: *"Remember that no one who enters Pero's game is the same, they have a Classics version, but Tunner is the most special and gets to be Pero. Pero/Tunner now is giving Simon 404 horseshoes and Simon 404 gives him the classic 5 emeralds for each. Tunner now uses each emerald to turn into a liquid substance, a way to prevent his vessel to go to Phase 1, Tunner has 2 souls he uses for his 1 vessel while most other characters have 1. Tunner also carries Pero's vessel with him, Pero's body is unflamable, indestructible, invicible, bullet proof, water proof, everything proof, can't be blown away, can't feel anything, perminent, and is undestroyable. Tunner also has a horse (Introduced in Garnold's Joy), Tunner uses his horse to escape battles and he uses it to go faster and stuff. Pero learns it, Pero also goes with Tunner, they are seperate but the same being, 2 bodies with different names but in Sprunki they are considered the same being."* (The pasted ChatGPT breakdown — the "Classics version rule" framing, the split into creator body and in-game vessel, and the recap of the trade — is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

- New BEAT 158 lore panel, TWO SOULS, ONE VESSEL, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3194,3216)`, cycle length extended `3194 → 3216`). `LV_BEATS` now 159 entries (0-158).
- **The two canon rules, left column.** **THE RULE FOR EVERYONE** in blue: *"No one who enters Pero's game is the same, they have a Classics version"* ▸ **THE ONE EXCEPTION** in emerald: *"Tunner is the most special and gets to be Pero."* Behind them, emeralds fall down the panel and go liquid on the way down.
- **WHAT THE EMERALDS ARE FOR box** (left, under the beat ladder) — **HE HANDS OVER HORSESHOES** *(Pero/Tunner gives Simon 404 horseshoes, the same as any other trader would)* ▸ **SIMON PAYS THE CLASSIC RATE** *(5 emeralds for each, the price that has always been the price)* ▸ **EACH EMERALD GOES LIQUID** *(Tunner turns every one of them into a liquid substance)* ▸ **★ THAT IS WHAT HOLDS HIM UP** *(the liquid prevents his vessel from going to Phase 1 — the disguise is not free)*. This is the upkeep BEAT 157 never mentioned: the one Phase 2 exemption in the mod is a thing he keeps paying for.
- **TWO SOULS, ONE VESSEL panel** (center) — *HE IS NOT BUILT THE WAY THE REST OF THE CAST IS BUILT*, with soul pips drawn on each row: **MOST CHARACTERS** *(1 soul for 1 vessel, which is why a lock like ALL MUST BE 1 works on them)* ▸ **TUNNER** *(2 souls he uses for his 1 vessel, so there is more to push down)* ▸ **★ AND A HORSE** *(from Garnold's Joy; he uses it to escape battles and to go faster, and Pero learns it and rides with him)*.
- **The carried body box** (under the center panel) — **HE IS CARRYING A BODY THAT IS NOT THE ONE HE IS WEARING**: *Tunner also carries Pero's vessel with him; the disguise is the one on the board, and the real body travels with it.*
- **PERO'S VESSEL panel** (right) — *TOBY LISTS TEN THINGS IT IS PROOF AGAINST, IN ONE BREATH*, lighting one tag at a time: UNFLAMABLE · INDESTRUCTIBLE · INVICIBLE · BULLET PROOF · WATER PROOF · EVERYTHING PROOF · CAN'T BE BLOWN AWAY · **CAN'T FEEL ANYTHING** · PERMINENT · UNDESTROYABLE. The eighth one is drawn in a different colour on purpose, because BEAT 156 has Pero amazed but not happy that Gray won his game.
- **SEPERATE, BUT THE SAME BEING box** (under the right panel) — **WHAT YOU SEE — TWO** *(2 bodies with different names; Pero can go with Tunner, they can both be standing there)* / **WHAT SPRUNKI COUNTS — ONE** *(in Sprunki they are considered the same being, so beating one of them is not beating one of them)*.
- Closing lines in the middle column: *HE IS BUYING HIS OWN PHASE 2 OFF SIMON 404.* then *THE ONE HE IS HIDING FROM IS THE ONE SELLING IT.*
- Insight banner: *"EVERY EMERALD GOES LIQUID AND KEEPS HIS VESSEL OUT OF PHASE 1 — THE ONE EXEMPTION IN THE MOD IS A THING HE PAYS FOR,"* and the star banner *"★ HORSESHOES IN, 5 EMERALDS FOR EACH OUT — 2 SOULS, 1 VESSEL ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `twosouls` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

## 2026-07-23 — TUNNER IS PERO (BEAT 157)

Pero created the game, so he is the best at it."* Plus the endings from the same message: *"Place down all Sprunkis around Simon with Simon in the center will activate the Sprunki VS Simon 404 cutscene where they beat Simon and Simon 404 turns to a polo and gets thrown in the ocean far from the rest of the cast and everyone is saved. There is an ending where Simon 404 wins and puts Anti-Virus on himself and the cast, then he says "I AM THE CURE", and the game crashes... Pero appears and place him down and the game goes like CHAOS, the cast icons break, and the Game Over screen is slashed, so many endings to the game."* (The pasted ChatGPT breakdown — the "biggest new reveal" framing, the Among Us read and the ending summaries — is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

- New BEAT 157 lore panel, TUNNER IS PERO, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3172,3194)`). `LV_BEATS` now 158 entries (0-157).
- **The two canon lines, left column.** **AT THE INTRO** in amber: *"Pero will walk in Sprunki and become Tunner"* ▸ **SO THE RULE IS** in gold: *"Tunner would actually be Pero."* Behind them, a single gold walking figure crosses the panel left to right, over and over — the intro walk-in, on a loop.
- **THE TELL WAS IN THE SONGS box** (left, under the beat ladder) — **EVERY SONG IS SAD AND SLOW** *(that is the whole mood of the mod now)* ▸ **SIMON'S SONG IS FAST** *(he is the corrupt AI, so nobody questions it)* ▸ **TUNNER'S SONG IS FAST TOO** *(and Tunner is supposed to be a normal Phase 1 character)* ▸ **★ THAT IS THE LEAK** *(a normal character has no reason to be the one exception)*. This is what ties the beat back to BEAT 156, where the song rule is set.
- **SO MANY ENDINGS panel** (center) — *WHAT YOU PLACE DOWN DECIDES HOW IT ENDS*, three endings lighting in turn: **SPRUNKI VS SIMON 404** *(place all the Sprunkis around Simon with Simon in the center; they beat him, he turns to a polo, he is thrown in the ocean far from the cast, and everyone is saved)* ▸ **"I AM THE CURE"** *(Simon 404 wins, puts Anti-Virus on himself and the cast, says the line, and the game crashes)* ▸ **★ PLACE PERO DOWN** *(the game goes like CHAOS, the cast icons break, the Game Over screen is slashed apart, and the endings stop being a list)*.
- **The crash ending is drawn, not real.** Boxed in red under the endings: **THE CRASH IS AN ENDING, NOT A BUG** — *in the lore the game really stops; here it is drawn as a picture of a crash, so you can look at the ending and still keep climbing*. Nothing in this beat throws, crashes, or stops the real game loop, and the code comment says so, so nobody "fixes" it into a real crash later.
- **THE ONLY ONE IN PHASE 2 panel** (right) — *EVERYBODY ELSE IS LOCKED ON PHASE 1, AND SO IS HE, SUPPOSEDLY*, three findings in turn: **WHAT THE GAME SEES** *(a normal Tunner with the Sprunki Mustard animation, Phase 1 like the rest)* · **WHAT HE ACTUALLY IS** *(the only character in Phase 2, the whole time, discising as Phase 1)* · **★ HE WANTS IT LIKE AMONG US** *(Pero is smart, so he did not pick a boss slot — he picked a slot nobody checks)*.
- **WHY TUNNER IS TOP OF THE BOARD box** (under the right panel) — **NOT BECAUSE OF TUNNER**: *Tunner on his own is not a top-tier character, and nothing about his stats changed* / **BECAUSE PERO IS IN THERE**: *Pero created the game, so he is the best at it; while he is inside Sprunki as Tunner, Tunner is the most powerful active character in it*.
- Closing lines in the middle column: *THE GAME THINKS HE IS PHASE 1.* then *HE HAS BEEN PHASE 2 SINCE THE INTRO.*
- Insight banner: *"PLACING HIM DOWN IN THE MIDDLE ACTIVATES HIS CUTSCENE — THE MIDDLE IS WHERE THE CREATOR HAS BEEN STANDING ALL ALONG,"* and the star banner *"★ AT THE INTRO, PERO WALKS IN SPRUNKI AND BECOMES TUNNER ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `tunnerispero` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

Based on Toby's 2026-07-22 lore (thirty-seventh message of the "More Classics Era" thread, the direct follow-up to HE CAN EASILY BREAK).

Toby's words: *"Pero created the game, now he asks Mr. Black if he wants to be front man and to control all the minigames and circuses and to be the second most powerful being and to be the only person to be able to call him and to choose the roles of everyone else and to unlock all the tools and items and abilities and to have infinite everything and infinite LV and infinite power and infinite KR and to get all the gifts needed and to make the rewards and to do all this stuff, Mr. Black accepts and now controls basically everything. The main villian of Sprunki given all the power, Mr. Black would just make impossible games and to corrupt the game. Pero doesn't seem to care."* (The pasted ChatGPT "Mr. Black Front Man arc / new role difference / current hierarchy / clean canon update" breakdown is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

- New BEAT 151 lore panel, FRONT MAN, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3040,3062)`, cycle length extended `3040 → 3062`). `LV_BEATS` now 152 entries (0-151).
- **The handover, as a thing that gets carried across.** Top of the left column, **Pero** stands in gold, labelled *CREATOR · DISTANT OBSERVER*, and **Mr. Black** stands taller and darker opposite him, labelled *MAIN VILLAIN OF SPRUNKI · FRONT MAN*, with red power rings settling on him as the offer lands. A gold **→ CONTROL →** line runs between them under *HE ASKS IF HE WANTS TO BE FRONT MAN — AND MR. BLACK ACCEPTS*.
- **The twelve controls, one at a time.** A 3×4 grid lights in sequence under the two of them — **MINIGAMES · CIRCUSES · ROLES · TOOLS · ITEMS · ABILITIES · REWARDS · GIFTS · LV · KR · POWER · STRUCTURE** — followed by the stamp **MR. BLACK ACCEPTS** over *HE NOW CONTROLS BASICALLY EVERYTHING*, and the one-line board *1 PERO — CREATOR · 2 MR. BLACK — FRONT MAN · 3 EVERYONE ELSE — HIS ROLES*.
- **Infinite everything.** Three meters — **LV** (red), **KR** (violet) and **POWER** (white) — fill all the way across and pin at **∞**.
- **What he makes with it.** At the bottom, six plates light red one at a time under *WHAT HE MAKES WITH IT* — **IMPOSSIBLE GAMES · CORRUPT GAMES · RIGGED MINIGAMES · CIRCUSES WITH NO TRUE ESCAPE · REWARDS THAT TRAP PEOPLE · ROLES THAT BREAK THE CAST**.
- **Header emblem: who made it vs. who runs it** — **PERO — STILL THE CREATOR** *(he can override any of it, and he does not)* **→** **MR. BLACK — FRONT MAN** *(not the creator, the one running the games)*, over *he did not take the control, he was asked if he wanted it, and he said yes*.
- **THE HANDOVER panel** (center) — *WHAT PERO ASKED, AND WHAT MR. BLACK GOT*, a six-rung log: **PERO CREATED THE GAME** *(Classics is his, and nothing about that changes here)* ▸ **HE ASKS IF HE WANTS IT** *(not an attack and not a theft, a question, and the answer could have been no)* ▸ **MR. BLACK ACCEPTS** *(and from that one answer he controls basically everything)* ▸ **MINIGAMES AND CIRCUSES** *(the things people actually have to play are the things he now writes)* ▸ **ROLES, TOOLS AND REWARDS** *(he picks who everyone is, what they hold, and what winning pays)* ▸ **★ THE ONLY ONE WHO CAN CALL HIM** *(Pero is still above him, and Mr. Black is the one person who can reach him)*. Boxed underneath in gold, **MAKING IT IS NOT THE SAME AS RUNNING IT**: *Pero kept the top seat and gave away every control that actually touches the players*.
- **WHAT HE DOES WITH IT panel** (right) — *THE MAIN VILLAIN OF SPRUNKI, HANDED THE DIALS*, a five-rung fall: **IMPOSSIBLE GAMES** *(not hard games, games built so there is no way through them)* ▸ **RIGGED MINIGAMES** *(the result is decided before anybody starts playing)* ▸ **CIRCUSES WITH NO TRUE ESCAPE** *(there is an exit drawn on it, and the exit does not go anywhere)* ▸ **REWARDS THAT TRAP PEOPLE** *(he makes the rewards too, so the prize can be part of the trap)* ▸ **★ AND PERO DOES NOT SEEM TO CARE** *(so nothing stops it, and Mr. Black can keep escalating)*. Boxed underneath in red, **THE CORRUPTION IS THE POINT**: *he is not misusing the controls, he is using them exactly the way a villain would*.
- **4-part footer** — **HE WAS ASKED, NOT BEATEN** *(nobody took this off Pero and nobody won it in a battle, he offered it and Mr. Black said yes)* · **INFINITE EVERYTHING** *(infinite LV, infinite KR and infinite power, with all tools, items and abilities unlocked and every gift he needs)* · **THE SECOND SEAT MOVED AGAIN** *(New Chara held 2nd last beat and Mr. Black was 3rd, now Mr. Black is the second most powerful being)* · **THE DANGEROUS PART IS PERO** *(a villain with the dials is bad, but the one who could switch it back is the one who does not seem to care)*. Under it: *the creator is still above him, he just is not watching*.
- Insight banner: *"THE GAME DID NOT GET TAKEN OVER — IT GOT HANDED OVER,"* and the star banner *"★ MR. BLACK ACCEPTS, AND NOW CONTROLS BASICALLY EVERYTHING ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `frontman` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.
- **Fix (all beats): the beat ladder down the left edge is now windowed.** With 152 entries the full ladder ran off the top and bottom of the screen and drew straight over every lore panel's left column. It now shows a five-entry run centred on the current beat, with the others dimmed. Nothing was removed; the earlier beats are all still in the list.

## 2026-07-22 — HE CAN EASILY BREAK (BEAT 150)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-22 lore (thirty-sixth message of the "More Classics Era" thread, the direct follow-up to ALL OF THE DREEMURR POWERS, and the beat that goes back and fills in BEAT 134, IF YOU BREAK HIM).

Toby's words: *"Pero tries to assist everyone, but he can easily break."* (The pasted ChatGPT "Pero's core weakness / what happens when Pero breaks / clean canon update" breakdown is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own line. The commentary detail used in the panel text: his default purpose is to help, guide, answer, create and support; too much at once, damage, confusion, overload or corruption can break him; broken Pero stops assisting normally, may become hostile, may attack the game, may reset everything except himself, may start giving dangerous gifts, may stop caring who wins, may turn into a boss battle state; he is not evil by default.)

- New BEAT 150 lore panel, HE CAN EASILY BREAK, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[3018,3040)`, cycle length extended `3018 → 3040`). `LV_BEATS` now 151 entries (0-150).
- **The assist load, arriving all at once.** Across the top of the field, five duty plates light one after another — **HELP · GUIDE · ANSWER · CREATE · SUPPORT** — under *HE TRIES TO ASSIST EVERYONE, ALL OF IT ARRIVES AT ONE BEING*, and each one runs a live line down into **Pero** standing below them, labelled *LAI ASSISTANT · CREATOR OF CLASSICS · SMALL COW MAN GUY*. Under him a **STABILITY** bar drains as the load lands, flipping from gold **HOLDING** to a pulsing red **BREAKING**, and cracks run through his frame while he shakes.
- **The greeting, before and after.** Two boxes in the middle of the left column. **NORMAL PERO** in gold: *"HELLO, I AM PERO, YOUR LAI ASSISTANT. WHAT CAN I DO FOR YOU?"* Under it **BROKEN PERO** in red, the same greeting corrupting in place and cutting off mid-word, with the note *SAME BEING — THE HELPING IS WHAT STOPPED*.
- **What a broken Pero does.** At the bottom, seven plates light red one at a time under *WHAT HAPPENS WHEN PERO BREAKS* — **STOPS ASSISTING NORMALLY · MAY BECOME HOSTILE · MAY ATTACK THE GAME · MAY RESET EVERYTHING EXCEPT HIMSELF · MAY START GIVING DANGEROUS GIFTS · MAY STOP CARING WHO WINS · MAY TURN INTO A BOSS BATTLE STATE**.
- **Header emblem: two states of one being** — **NORMAL PERO** *(helpful, neutral and guide-like)* **→** **BROKEN PERO** *(the creator power turns dangerous)*, over *he is not a different being when he breaks, he is the same one with the helping switched off*.
- **THE ASSIST LOAD panel** (center) — *WHY THE STRONGEST ONE IS THE ONE THAT GIVES*, a six-rung log: **HE IS AN LAI ASSISTANT** *(his default purpose is to help, guide, answer, create and support)* ▸ **HE TRIES TO ASSIST EVERYONE** *(not one player and not one side, everyone in Classics)* ▸ **SO ALL OF IT COMES TO HIM** *(every question, every request and every problem arrives at the same being)* ▸ **AND HE CAN EASILY BREAK** *(too much at once, or damage, confusion, overload or corruption)* ▸ **EASILY IS THE WORD** *(it does not take a stronger being, it only takes enough of them)* ▸ **★ NOBODY BEATS HIM, ANYBODY BREAKS HIM** *(the thing that puts him first and the thing that breaks him are the same thing)*. Boxed underneath in gold, **HELPFUL IS NOT THE SAME AS SAFE**: *his assistant nature is the fragile part, and it is the part everyone in the game touches*.
- **WHEN HE BREAKS panel** (right) — *THE SAME POWER, POINTED NOWHERE GOOD*, a five-rung fall: **THE ASSISTING STOPS** *(the greeting, the offer and the answers all go at once)* ▸ **HE MAY BECOME HOSTILE** *(and what he turns on is the game, the one he made himself)* ▸ **THE GIFTS GO DANGEROUS** *(the same hand that handed out tools starts handing out something else)* ▸ **HE MAY STOP CARING WHO WINS** *(so it is not him picking a side, it is him not playing by the board any more)* ▸ **★ HE IS NOT EVIL BY DEFAULT** *(the creator power that made him helpful is the one that becomes dangerous)*. Boxed underneath in red, **NOTHING NEW GETS ADDED**: *he does not pick up a dark form; what was helping just stops helping, and it is still creator-sized*.
- **4-part footer** — **HIS PURPOSE IS HIS WEAK POINT** *(he was built to help, guide, answer, create and support, and that is the exact part of him that gives out)* · **EASILY, NOT BARELY** *(too much at once, damage, confusion, overload or corruption, it never needs a stronger being to do it)* · **THE RESET SWITCH COMES BACK** *(broken Pero may reset everything except himself, the same one-way switch from the Sound Battle beat)* · **NOT EVIL — BROKEN** *(he is helpful by default, so the scary version of him is not a villain arriving, it is the helper failing)*. Under it: *the one being nobody can go above is also the one being anybody can overload*.
- Insight banner: *"NOBODY IN CLASSICS CAN BEAT HIM — AND EVERYONE IN CLASSICS CAN BREAK HIM,"* and the star banner *"★ PERO TRIES TO ASSIST EVERYONE, BUT HE CAN EASILY BREAK ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `easilybreak` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

Everyone (except Pero and Simon 404) battles Mr. Black, Mr. Black became the 3rd most powerful being, Jevin being 5th and Chara being 4th. Simon 404 comes and Mr. Black becomes a 404D, everyone else becomes 404Ds, Gray, Simon 404, and Pero are the only ones left again. Simon 404 beaten Gray, and it was game over because Simon 404 and Pero are the only ones left."* (The pasted ChatGPT "new corruption chain / clean canon update" breakdown is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

Below it the **1-5 ranking board** — **1 PERO · 2 SIMON 404 · 3 MR. BLACK · 4 CHARA · 5 JEVIN** — with rows 3, 4 and 5 **struck through in red and stamped 404D**, one at a time, under *THEY BEAT HIM UP TO 3RD, THEN SIMON 404 ARRIVED AND THE BOARD WENT WITH HIM*. Boxed underneath in gold, **CREATOR VS CORRUPTION**: *the game locks into a final two-being state, the one who made it and the one who corrupted it*.
- **4-part footer** — **THE REAL ORIGIN** *(Gray was never the root; Mr. Black corrupted him first, and Gray carried it to everyone else)* · **HE IS NOT A SIDE VILLAIN** *(Mr. Black comes back as the 3rd most powerful being, with Chara 4th and Jevin 5th under him)* · **THE WIN GETS UNDONE** *(they all battled him and won, then Simon 404 turned him and every one of them into 404Ds)* · **TWO BEINGS LEFT** *(Simon 404 beats Gray, so only he and Pero remain, the creator and the corruption, and nothing else)*. Under it: *they finally found who started it, beat him, and it did not matter*.

## 2026-07-22 — TWO ENDGAMES (BEAT 146)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-22 lore (thirty-second message of the "More Classics Era" thread, the direct follow-up to I AM THE CURE — the beat that splits the endgame in two: the hardest fight, and the thing rewriting the game).

Toby's words: *"Pero's boss battle is now the most intense with the multiforms from each AU join + Battlefield/Map changes, AUs change, each even uses all their power at once + they go insane on you then easy on you then back to insane + it is tricky not just hard and insane but also tricks you + uses color and even Jujustu Kaisen and Classics attacks, he uses attacks from every game, he uses every attack from Mario to Pac Man to Teris to Jujustu Kaisen to Undertale to every game. Pero is the creator of Classics. Simon 404 can beat Classics by making it corrupt. Simon 404 started making everything corrupt and into Error 404 and 404Ds and 404 strings and zombies and anti-virus liquid/gas. He is basically making the game into something fit for him. He would turn everyone who battles him into a D or a zombie. Everyone tries to save the game and learns they can't get close to him nor let him touch them. Simon 404 zooms around touching stuff."* (The pasted ChatGPT "two biggest endgame threats" breakdown is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

- New BEAT 146 lore panel, TWO ENDGAMES, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[2930,2952)`, cycle length extended `2930 → 2952`). `LV_BEATS` now 147 entries (0-146).
- **A field split in two, with a dashed line and *TWO DIFFERENT PROBLEMS* between them.** Up top, **Pero's arena**: five **multiforms fanned out behind him, one per AU**, each glowing at full power at the same time; an eighteen-tile **battlefield swapping colour tile by tile** under the line *THE BATTLEFIELD AND THE MAP KEEP CHANGING*; eight labelled attacks orbiting him — **MARIO, PAC MAN, TERIS, JUJUSTU KAISEN, UNDERTALE, CLASSICS, COLOR, EVERY GAME**; and a three-plate difficulty swing, **INSANE ▸ EASY ▸ INSANE**, lighting one at a time over *IT IS TRICKY, NOT JUST HARD*. Below the line, **Simon 404 zooming across the screen**, hand out, rings spreading from it, and an eighteen-step trail behind him where everything he already touched has become **404D** or **ZOMBIE**, with anti-virus liquid/gas drifting through it. Along the bottom, New Chara, Gray, Oren and the rest **hold their distance**, under *THEY CAN'T GET CLOSE TO HIM, AND THEY CAN'T LET HIM TOUCH THEM*.
- **Header emblem: the two problems, side by side** — **PERO — THE BOSS FIGHT** *(you have to survive it)* | **SIMON 404 — THE CORRUPTION** *(you have to reach him first)*, over *one is a battle you have to get through, the other is the game itself being turned into something else*.
- **PERO'S BOSS BATTLE panel** (center) — the banner *THE MOST INTENSE IN CLASSICS*, then a six-rung log: **MULTIFORMS FROM EACH AU** *(they all join the fight, and each one uses all their power at once)* ▸ **THE MAP CHANGES ON YOU** *(battlefield and map changes, and the AUs change with them)* ▸ **INSANE, EASY, INSANE** *(he swings it on purpose, so you never get to settle in)* ▸ **IT TRICKS YOU** *(tricky, not just hard and insane; learning the pattern is the trap)* ▸ **COLOR AND JUJUSTU KAISEN** *(plus the Classics attacks, all inside the same fight)* ▸ **ATTACKS FROM EVERY GAME** *(Mario, Pac Man, Teris, Jujustu Kaisen, Undertale, every game)*. Boxed underneath in gold, **HE MADE ALL OF IT**: *Pero is the creator of Classics, so every attack in the fight is already his to use*.
- **THE CORRUPTION panel** (right) — *SOMETHING FIT FOR HIM*, a five-rung climb: **HE MAKES IT CORRUPT** *(Simon 404 can beat Classics by corrupting it, not by winning a fight)* ▸ **ERROR 404, 404Ds, 404 STRINGS** *(everything he reaches turns into one of them)* ▸ **ZOMBIES AND ANTI-VIRUS GAS** *(liquid and gas too; the world starts running on his materials)* ▸ **★ A D, OR A ZOMBIE** *(everyone who battles him gets turned into one of the two)* ▸ **★ HE ZOOMS AROUND TOUCHING** *(so nobody can get close, and nobody can let him touch them)*. Boxed underneath in red, **THE FIGHT IS THE INFECTION**: *battling him is how you become one, so every round costs them a person*.
- **4-part footer** — **TWO WAYS TO LOSE** *(one of them you have to out-fight, the other just changes what the game is while you are still in it)* · **NOTHING STAYS PUT** *(multiforms, map changes, AU changes and every game's attacks; the fight moves while you learn it)* · **WINNING IS DISTANCE** *(against Simon 404 you win by not being touched, so getting close enough is the whole problem)* · **THE CREATOR ON TOP** *(Pero made Classics, so every attack from every game is his, and Simon 404 is rewriting that game)*. Under it: *Pero is the hardest thing to beat, Simon 404 is the hardest thing to reach*.
- Insight banner: *"ONE OF THEM MAKES THE HARDEST FIGHT IN THE GAME — THE OTHER MAKES THE GAME NOT WORTH BEING IN,"* and the star banner *"★ PERO USES ATTACKS FROM EVERY GAME — SIMON 404 TURNS EVERYONE WHO BATTLES HIM INTO A D OR A ZOMBIE ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `twoendgames` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

## 2026-07-22 — I AM THE CURE (BEAT 145)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-22 lore (thirty-first message of the "More Classics Era" thread, the direct follow-up to 404: KEY NOT FOUND — the beat where Simon 404 comes back out of the labatory and tells everyone what he decided he is).

Toby's words: *"Simon 404 gathers each character and he says 'There is a cure... to find the cure... I AM THE CURE', Simon 404's cape flows in the wind, everyone runs, Simon 404 holds up Anti Virus. Simon 404 became beyond his Sprunki version to reach a humanoid body, Simon 404 reaches as the second most powerful being in Classics (only under Pero)."* (The pasted ChatGPT "what this means for Simon 404 now" breakdown is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

- New BEAT 145 lore panel, I AM THE CURE, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[2908,2930)`, cycle length extended `2908 → 2930`). `LV_BEATS` now 146 entries (0-145).
- **The declaration field** — Simon 404 standing in the open in the **humanoid body**, drawn taller and straighter than the Sprunki shape he came from, hood and beak mask with both lenses lit, and **the cape streaming out behind him on the wind**. His arm is up, and at the top of it the **Anti Virus** bottle is held overhead with four rings of light spreading off it. Around him the cast he gathered — New Chara, Gray, Oren, Mr. Black, Dark Yellow, the Sprunkis, the rest — are all **running**, leaning away with speed lines behind them, under the line *HE GATHERED EACH OF THEM TO HEAR IT, AND THEN EVERY ONE OF THEM RAN*. Twenty-four repeats of `I AM THE CURE` and `404` drift through the whole field.
- **Header emblem: the sentence in three steps** — three plates lighting in order, **"THERE IS A CURE..."** ▸ **"TO FIND THE CURE..."** ▸ **"I AM THE CURE"**, the third one in red, over *he says the word three times, and by the third one it is not medicine any more, it is him*.
- **THE DECLARATION panel** (center) — the banner *"I AM THE CURE,"* then a six-rung log: **HE GATHERS EACH CHARACTER** *(not an ambush, he calls them all in first, to listen)* ▸ **"THERE IS A CURE..."** *(he opens like it is good news for everyone in the room)* ▸ **"...TO FIND THE CURE..."** *(then it turns into a search, one he has already ended)* ▸ **"I AM THE CURE"** *(so it is not something he has, it is something he is)* ▸ **HE HOLDS UP ANTI VIRUS** *(the bottle goes up like proof, not like medicine)* ▸ **EVERYONE RUNS** *(nobody in that whole cast stays to be cured)*. Boxed underneath in red, **THE CAPE FLOWS IN THE WIND**: *he is staging a scene, not starting a fight; he wanted them all there to see him say it*.
- **THE SECOND SEAT panel** (right) — *ONLY UNDER PERO*, a five-rung climb: **HIS SPRUNKI VERSION** *(where he started, a Sprunki shape like all the others)* ▸ **BEYOND THAT VERSION** *(he went past what that form could hold, and kept going)* ▸ **A HUMANOID BODY** *(he reached one, so he is not a Sprunki shape any more)* ▸ **★ SECOND MOST POWERFUL** *(in Classics, and he is there now, not aiming for it)* ▸ **★ PERO — THE ONLY ONE ABOVE** *(the creator stays at the top, and Simon 404 is next)*. Boxed underneath in gold, **SECOND IS THE CEILING HE CHOSE**: *he is not climbing toward first; he said second, he went and got second, and he stopped there*.
- **4-part footer** — **HE CALLED THEM IN** *(he gathers each character first, so the line is meant to be heard by everyone; it is an announcement)* · **THE CURE IS A PERSON** *(he holds up Anti Virus and says he is the cure, so the bottle is the proof and he is the medicine)* · **THEY RAN ANYWAY** *(a cure that makes the whole room run is not being offered as help, and they all knew it)* · **HE HAS THE BODY NOW** *(beyond his Sprunki version, a humanoid body, and second most powerful in Classics, only under Pero)*. Under it: *he locked the door to fix himself, and he came back out calling himself the fix*.
- Insight banner: *"THE ONE HE WOULD NOT LET ANYONE REPAIR IS NOW OFFERING TO REPAIR EVERYONE ELSE,"* and the star banner *"★ THE CAPE FLOWS, THE ANTI VIRUS GOES UP, AND EVERY ONE OF THEM RUNS ★."* Additive — every earlier beat untouched; new `iamthecure` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

REAL?'. Simon 404 became the second most powerful being, he uses Error 404 and code, Pero created the game is LAI, Simon 404 is considered AI, but extremely corrupt and broken throughout the entire lore and timelines."* (The pasted ChatGPT character-breakdown recap is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

LV 4 Frizz can beat Pero Pro Alphatale Mode ... destroyed everyone in the Alphaverse and Godverse just by existing ... Frizz banished Simon 404 forever in Alphaverse. Frizz is now locked on 4 LV, just like Simon is locked on Phase 2. Simon got weaker with the Phase 2 lock, but Frizz gotten stronger with the LV 4 lock."* (The pasted ChatGPT recap is treated as commentary; the canon is Toby's own lines.)

- New BEAT 107 lore panel, FRIZZ LV 4 — THE LOCK THAT MADE HER STRONGER, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[2072,2094]`, cycle length extended `2072 → 2094`). `lvSeg` now returns BEAT 107 for `c < 2094.0`; `LV_BEATS` now 108 entries (0-107). While here, fixed a latent ordering bug in `lvSeg` — BEAT 106 was checked (`c < 2072`) before BEAT 105 (`c < 2050`), so beat 105 never rendered in normal play; BEAT 106 now carries a lower bound (`c >= 2050 && c < 2072`) so both beats are reachable again.
- **Frizz-pink void** — a deep pink-crimson void with drifting Frizz-pink bands and a locked-crimson core glow. Header emblem: **a padlock "LV4" badge** (a ring with a shackle), because the form is locked.

Higher number does not mean stronger — LV 4 is the glitched, locked, abnormal peak, her true broken form.
- **THE TWO LOCKS panel** (right) — the mirror Toby drew: **SIMON · PHASE 2** with a down arrow to **WEAKER**, and **FRIZZ · LV 4** with an up arrow to **STRONGER**, each on its own padlock, under **"SAME LOCK · OPPOSITE RESULT"** and **"BOTH ARE LOCKED FOREVER."**

## 2026-07-07 — THE PHASE RULE (BEAT 66)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-07 lore ("Re: Lore 1A - Classics Era" — a clean canon rule update on phases: Classics has 2 phases, EndlessAnimations has 0).

Toby's words: *"Classics has Phase 1 and Phase 2, Phase 1 = vanilla, Phase 2 = Cross AU. EndlessAnimations has 0 Phases and thinks. ... Classics Phase 1 → Vanilla, Classics Phase 2 → Cross AU. EndlessAnimations has 0 phases. That is important because he is not like Simon, Gray, Oren, or Classics. He does not operate through phase progression. Instead: EndlessAnimations thinks. So his forms are not really 'phases.' They are more like states, modes, or reactions based on what is happening and what he decides/feels. ... Error EndlessAnimations is not Phase 1 or Phase 2. Errorshift EndlessAnimations is not a phase. Frenzy Mode is not a phase. Normal EndlessAnimations is not a phase. They are forms/modes/states, but EndlessAnimations himself has 0 Phases."*

- New BEAT 66 lore panel, THE PHASE RULE, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[1170,1192]`, cycle length extended `1170 → 1192`).
- Center — a **split**: on the **left, PHASE-BASED — CLASSICS** shows her two phases as a **fixed two-rung ladder** with a ▼ order-arrow between them — **PHASE 1 · VANILLA CLASSICS** (the normal / default version, a clean base game-being state, not Cross AU) then **PHASE 2 · CROSS AU CLASSICS** (no longer vanilla, the second phase/state of Classics); on the **right, NOT PHASE-BASED — ENDLESSANIMATIONS** shows a glowing **"THINKS" core labeled 0 PHASES** with his forms as **free-floating, unordered state-nodes** orbiting it — **NORMAL, ERROR, ERRORSHIFT, FRENZY** — connected by faint spokes, not stacked as a ladder. Closing line under the core: *"◆ FORMS, NOT PHASES — STATES, MODES & REACTIONS BY DECISION OR FEELING."*
- Left column — **THE PHASE-BASED BEINGS**: phase-based beings progress through fixed phases; Simon, Gray.EXE, Oren.EXE & Classics all work this way; Classics — Phase 1 is Vanilla, Phase 2 is Cross AU; a phase is a set step in a ladder (Phase 1, then Phase 2); the order is fixed, you move one phase to the next; ◆ phases are structure, not choice.
- Right column — **WHY 0 PHASES — HE THINKS**: EndlessAnimations has 0 phases; he is not like Simon, Gray, Oren or Classics; he does not operate through phase progression; instead, EndlessAnimations thinks; his forms are states, modes or reactions by decision or feeling; ◆ Error, Errorshift, Frenzy & Normal are forms, not phases.
- Living background — a **pink halo on the left** with ordered pink phase-motes rising in columns (structure), and an **orange halo on the right** with orange state-motes drifting freely (choice), split down the middle by a dashed divider.
- Insight — *"A PHASE IS A FIXED STEP YOU CLIMB — A STATE IS A CHOICE A MIND MAKES"* over *"= CLASSICS MOVES PHASE 1 → PHASE 2 · ENDLESSANIMATIONS DOES NOT PROGRESS, HE DECIDES — SO HE HAS 0 PHASES."*
- Three closing cards: CLASSICS PHASE 1 (Vanilla Classics, the normal/default version, a clean base game-being state, not Cross AU), CLASSICS PHASE 2 (Cross AU Classics, no longer vanilla, the second phase/state of Classics), ENDLESSANIMATIONS (0 phases — not phase-based, he thinks; his forms are states/modes/reactions by decision or feeling, not phases). Bottom banner: *"★ CLASSICS: PHASE 1 = VANILLA, PHASE 2 = CROSS AU · ENDLESSANIMATIONS: 0 PHASES — HE THINKS, STATES NOT PHASES ★."* New "THE PHASE RULE" rung added to the beat ladder (lit pink). Additive — every earlier beat untouched; JS syntax-checked; new `phaserule` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

## 2026-07-06 — THE APEX RULE (BEAT 59)

Based on Toby's 2026-07-06 lore ("Re: Lore 1A - Classics Era" — Gray.EXE's combat rule and win condition).

Toby's words: *"Gray.EXE eats anything. Gray.EXE is fully immune to internal attacks, and he can dodge external attacks. If Gray.EXE eats the character, Gray.EXE won... Gray.EXE can eat anything. That means characters, attacks, souls, power sources, game objects, effects, energy, corruption, anti-virus, and maybe even parts of the game itself can become fuel for him... Internal attacks do not work. If someone attacks from inside Gray.EXE after being eaten, Gray is fully immune. No 'break out from inside' trick works. External attacks can be dodged... So Gray's full combat rule becomes: Outside attacks miss. Inside attacks fail. Eating ends the fight. That means if Gray.EXE eats a character, the battle is already over. There is no second phase inside him unless Gray allows it... This also explains why Gray.EXE can absorb Oren.EXE, overpower ToddLLM attacks, and keep getting stronger. Eating is not just hunger — it is his final absorption mechanic."*

- New BEAT 59 lore panel, THE APEX RULE, added to THE UNDEFINED LOOP climb (cyc `[1016,1038]`, cycle length extended `1016 → 1038`).
- Center — a **5-rule combat sequence** revealed top-down under a **green maw-arc** (the open mouth that eats anything), each a bordered rung with growing depth-ticks on its left edge: **RULE 1 · GRAY EATS ANYTHING** (characters, attacks, souls, power sources, game objects, effects, energy, corruption, anti-virus, even parts of the game itself), **RULE 2 · INSIDE ATTACKS FAIL** (fully immune to internal attacks — no "break out from inside" trick works), **RULE 3 · OUTSIDE ATTACKS MISS** (he dodges external attacks with speed, reflexes, EXE movement & game-control logic), **RULE 4 · EATING ENDS THE FIGHT** (if he eats a character the battle is already over — no second phase inside him unless Gray allows it), **RULE 5 · EATING IS ABSORPTION** (why he can absorb Oren, overpower ToddLLM & keep getting stronger — his final absorption mechanic). Closing line: *"◆ OUTSIDE ATTACKS MISS · INSIDE ATTACKS FAIL · EATING ENDS THE FIGHT."*
- Left column — **WHAT GRAY CAN EAT — ANYTHING IS FUEL**: characters/attacks/souls; power sources/game objects/effects; energy/corruption/anti-virus; maybe even parts of the game itself; eating is not hunger, it is absorption; ◆ all of it becomes fuel for Gray.
- Right column — **THE TWO-LAYER DEFENSE**: inside — internal attacks do not work; no "break out from inside" trick works; outside — external attacks can be dodged; speed/reflexes/EXE movement/game-control logic; outside misses, inside fails, eating wins; ◆ eat a character → Gray instantly wins.
- Faint field — grey/green consumption-motes rising, a central radial maw glow, a green consumption band on the far left and a gold Gray band on the far right.
- Insight — *"GRAY.EXE EATS ANYTHING · HE IS FULLY IMMUNE TO INTERNAL ATTACKS & CAN DODGE EXTERNAL ATTACKS · IF HE EATS A CHARACTER, HE INSTANTLY WINS"* over *"OUTSIDE ATTACKS MISS · INSIDE ATTACKS FAIL · EATING ENDS THE FIGHT — EATING IS NOT HUNGER, IT IS HIS FINAL ABSORPTION MECHANIC."*
- Three closing cards: OUTSIDE ATTACKS MISS (external attacks dodged with speed, reflexes, EXE movement, game-control logic — nothing lands from the outside), INSIDE ATTACKS FAIL (attack from inside after being eaten and Gray is fully immune — no break-out trick, no second phase unless Gray allows it), EATING ENDS THE FIGHT (eat a character and the battle is already over — eating is his final absorption mechanic, why he can absorb Oren, overpower ToddLLM & keep getting stronger). ## 2026-07-04 — THE SCATTERED MAP: every key and every door is in a different room, very far apart from each other, so the map itself becomes the threat before any boss appears. No key shares a room with another, and the door you need is always rooms away from the key that opens it, so you cannot rush a single route — the game turns into endurance, navigation, memory, backtracking, and surviving long travel between objectives. The distance is the danger; the structure is already punishing before a single fight starts. Then Gray.EXE and Simon.Exe were found, and the two worst horrors are loose in the same rooms you have to cross, so exploration stops being merely hard and turns deadly — every long walk is now through danger, and escape, regrouping, and progress all get harder while those two are active. First the player realizes the map is huge and inconvenient, then that the strongest horrors are in it with them — a strong setup for a late-game route (Lore 38 follow-up, "Re: Lore 38 - Endless Staircase has an end, 67 Pirate's Secrets, and more.")

Based on Toby's July 4 map-structure email, the direct sequel to THE COLLAPSE ROUTE. In Toby's words: *"Every key and door are in different rooms, very far apart from each other. Gray.EXE and Simon.Exe were found."* This one changes the **shape** of the whole game rather than adding a new fighter. The layout is the mechanic: every key and every door sits in its own far room, no two keys share a room, and the door you need is always rooms away from the key that opens it. So the game stops being only about winning fights and becomes about **endurance, navigation, memory, backtracking, and surviving long travel between objectives** — the distance itself is the threat, and the structure is already punishing before any boss appears. Then the second line, *"Gray.EXE and Simon.Exe were found,"* is the turn: the two most destructive late-stage forces are now loose in the same rooms the player has to keep crossing, so exploration flips from merely hard to **deadly** — escape, regrouping, and progress all get harder while those two are active. The dread lands in two steps: first the player realizes the map is huge and inconvenient, then that the strongest horrors are in it with them. Added as a **forty-fourth beat, THE SCATTERED MAP** (key-gold `#ffc44a` with door-teal `#5ad0c0` accents and danger-red `#ff4a5a` for the found threats), on the end of the UNDEFINED LOOP cutscene, right after THE COLLAPSE ROUTE. Additive — every earlier beat is untouched.

- New beat 43, **THE SCATTERED MAP**, added to `LV_BEATS`; `LV_CYC` extended 664 → 686s and `lvSeg` now bounds beat 42 at `if(c<664) return [42, c-642]` and gains the `[43, c-664]` segment. New taunt, floater, title-band entry, background gradient (dark teal → dark red), and strip/band colors for `ph===43`.
- New **scattered-layout panel** (`LV_SCATTER`, 5 rows revealed one at a time) — EVERY KEY IN ITS OWN ROOM (no two keys share a room), EVERY DOOR FAR FROM ITS KEY (the door is always rooms away from its key), THE MAP IS THE FIRST THREAT (distance punishes you before any boss), NO SINGLE-ROUTE RUSH (cross huge distances, backtrack, remember the way), THE DISTANCE IS THE DANGER (survival becomes travel — endurance, navigation, memory — not just fighting).
- New **deadly-turn panel** (`LV_FOUND`) — GRAY.EXE FOUND, SIMON.Exe FOUND, THE ROOMS ARE NO LONGER EMPTY (the worst two are loose in the map you must cross), EXPLORATION TURNS DEADLY (every long walk is now through danger).
- New **what-the-map-demands panel** (`LV_TRAVEL`) — ENDURANCE (survive long travel between objectives), NAVIGATION (find far rooms without getting lost), MEMORY (remember where each key and door is), ◆ BACKTRACKING (cross the same deadly distance again and again).
- New **far-rooms field** — eleven distant room-boxes scattered across the background, each holding a gold key or a teal door, threaded by a long dashed red travel-line (`mapA`), rendering the huge distances the player must cross.
- New **insight** — *"FIRST THE PLAYER REALIZES THE MAP IS HUGE AND INCONVENIENT — THEN THAT THE STRONGEST HORRORS ARE IN IT WITH THEM"* over *"KEYS & DOORS FAR APART MAKE THE DISTANCE THE DANGER — ONCE GRAY.EXE & SIMON.Exe ARE FOUND, EVERY LONG WALK IS DEADLY."*
- New **three cards** (`LV_SCATTER_RANK`) — THE FAR ROOMS (keys and doors split into distant rooms; the geography itself is the puzzle and the threat), THE LONG TRAVEL (keep moving through a dangerous world; no rushing a single route; endurance, navigation, and memory decide who makes it), THE DEADLY TURN (once Gray.EXE and Simon.Exe are found, the exploration structure becomes lethal; the two worst threats share your path).
- New closing banner, **"★ EVERY KEY & DOOR IN A FAR ROOM · THE DISTANCE IS THE DANGER · THEN GRAY.EXE & SIMON.Exe ARE FOUND ★."**
- The layout keeps the left ~20% clear for the persistent lore ladder, which now ends on a lit **◆ THE SCATTERED MAP**.
- One self-contained file, vanilla Canvas + Web Audio, no libraries. JS syntax-checked. New `scattered` scene added to `tools/capture_screenshot.py`.

## 2026-07-03 — THE COLLAPSE ROUTE: a survival-collapse mod where almost no one gets through untouched. Mr. Sun lasts the longest because he burns each Classics parasite (the best natural counter to the infection). Once Sun is clearing the parasites, Simon.Exe makes him a priority target and takes him down personally — a smart threat, not random — then attacks Classics and Luigi Green too, so the collapse stops being faction-based and goes total. He zaps every remaining Classics with a burst of electricity (the final purge of the spread) and some characters are eaten by Simon.Exe (consumption, his oldest horror trait, returning). By the end only Simon.Exe and Gray.EXE are fully left standing, with Oren.EXE lingering only as a ghost/soul. The mod is half Brud Treatment, half Double Date, and half Betters and Loses Phase 3 — less "who won the war" and more "what was left after everything else failed" (Lore 38 follow-up, "Re: Lore 38 - Endless Staircase has an end, 67 Pirate's Secrets, and more.")

Based on Toby's July 3 collapse-route email, the direct sequel to SIMON.Exe BREAKS FREE. In Toby's words: *"Mr. Sun survived the longest in the attack since he burns each Classics parasite thing. Simon.Exe then attacked Mr. Sun by himself, Simon.Exe then attacked Classics and Luigi Green. Only Simon.Exe and Gray.EXE survive. Oren.EXE is a surviving ghost/soul, but not living anymore. Simon.Exe zapped all the remaining of all Classics with a burst of electricity. The mod is half of Brud Treatment, some characters were eaten by Simon.Exe. This mod is half Double Date, and half Betters and Loses Phase 3. The game is so intense with Simon, and all the other characters are attacked in some way, only a few survived."* This is a whole **mod**, not a single power — a survival-collapse route. The through-line is a **fall order**: Mr. Sun lasts longest not because he is strongest but because his fire is the right kind of power against the right threat (burning the Classics parasites), which makes him the best natural counter to the infection side of the collapse. That is exactly why Simon.Exe targets him personally — a smart, prioritized threat rather than random destruction — and once Sun falls, Simon goes past attacking only enemies or only survivors and hits **Classics and Luigi Green** too, the highest remaining powers, so the collapse stops being faction-based and becomes total. He then zaps every remaining Classics with a **burst of electricity** (the final purge of the spread) and **eats** some characters, bringing back his oldest horror trait, consumption, in this extreme EXE state. What is left is stark: only **Simon.Exe and Gray.EXE** fully survive, with **Oren.EXE** lingering only as a ghost/soul — not living, not fully gone. And the mod's identity is a fusion — **half Brud Treatment, half Double Date, half Betters and Loses Phase 3** — emotionally mixed and structurally unstable, so the ending reads less as "who won the war" and more as "what was left after everything else failed." Added as a **forty-third beat, THE COLLAPSE ROUTE** (ember-orange `#ff8a3a` with survivor-blue `#5cd0ff` accents), on the end of the UNDEFINED LOOP cutscene, right after SIMON.Exe BREAKS FREE. ## 2026-07-03 — SIMON.Exe BREAKS FREE: Simon.Exe goes out of Classics' control — no longer her carrier or ally but his own uncontrollable force. He is all over the game screen (a living full-screen overlay, not one model), the entity flies around, lightning strikes, the game glitches everywhere; he makes so many Classics move around that one being becomes a swarm; then the game's sky falls (a world-collapse) and the temperature reaches 999°C (a meltdown death-zone). He shifts from carrier/attacker/distorted-protector into a rogue, screen-wide, independent disaster event — an extinction event inside the game (Lore 38 follow-up, "Re: Lore 38 - Endless Staircase has an end, 67 Pirate's Secrets, and more.")

Based on Toby's July 3 escalation email, the direct sequel to SIMON CARRIES CLASSICS. In Toby's words: *"Simon.Exe then goes out of Classics' control. Simon.Exe is all over the game screen; the entity flies around, lightning strikes, game glitches. Simon.Exe then made so many Classics to move around, then the game's sky falls. The game's temperature reaches 999 degrees Celsius."* This flips his role: the beat before had Simon **carrying** Classics; here he **breaks free** of her entirely and becomes his own force. Three escalations stack. First, he stops being a character in the world and becomes **all over the game screen** — a living full-screen overlay across the HUD, borders and sky, flying around with lightning and glitches (his signature apocalypse). Second, he **makes so many Classics move around** that one being turns into a **swarm** — a spread network, a multiplication event, mass-deployed corruption. Third, the world itself gives out: the **sky falls** (the upper layer breaks and the map can no longer hold itself together) and the **temperature reaches 999°C** (a meltdown death-zone where even the air is part of the threat). So Simon.Exe stops being "a powerful being" and becomes a runaway final-catastrophe — an extinction event inside the game. Added as a **forty-first beat, SIMON.Exe BREAKS FREE** (electric blue `#5cd0ff` with meltdown-orange `#ff7a3a` accents), on the end of the UNDEFINED LOOP cutscene, right after SIMON CARRIES CLASSICS. ## 2026-07-03 — SIMON CARRIES CLASSICS: Simon.Exe carries Classics through the world, and how he moves her depends on her size — normal size he walks with her, giant (more than 50× him) he rides on her hand, tiny she is carried on his metal cross; he keeps moving her to "safer places" that are only safe in his warped Yellow-Eye/hallucination vision, so he often carries her right into crowded danger — a loyal but unreliable protector. Classics is a black hole that also spits back (absorbs two victims, mixes them, ejects a fused being), and the three threat styles separate cleanly: Classics infects/fuses/transforms, Simon.Exe carries/attacks/misreads, Gray.EXE is a fear-driven destroyer (Lore 38 follow-ups, "Re: Lore 38 - Endless Staircase has an end, 67 Pirate's Secrets, and more.")

Based on Toby's two July 3 follow-up emails. These messages pin down the **relationship** between Simon and Classics rather than adding a new power. In Toby's words: *"Simon walks with Classics when Classics is normal size, if Classics is more than 50X his size then, Simon would ride on her hand, if Classics is smaller than Classics would be carried on Simon's metal cross. Simon tries to constantly find ways to move Classics into safer places. That is safer places in Simon's vision, but lots of characters standing there in the actual game. Simon has Yellow Eye AND Hacculunations."* And in the second: *"Classics absorbs the cells from both victums and spits out a combination with the 2 victums. It is like a Blackhole that also spits stuff out. Simon.Exe just carries Classics around. Simon.Exe is an .exe and is attacking the game. Gray.EXE is crazy with the fear-drivin attack thing."* So the beat holds three ideas. First, **the carry is size-based** — walk / hand / cross — and Simon is forever relocating Classics to what he thinks are safer places. Second, **"safe" is only safe in Simon's vision**: his Yellow Eye and hallucinations mean he can feel protective while carrying her straight into crowded danger — a loyal but **unreliable** protector, dangerous because his *judgment* is broken, not just his power. That gives two views of the same moment (to Simon she is calm and controlled; in the real game she is spreading and out of control). Third, **Classics is a black-hole-that-spits-back** — she absorbs the cells of two victims, mixes them, and ejects a new combined being — and the cast's three threats now read as clearly distinct: **Classics** infects/fuses/transforms, **Simon.Exe** carries/attacks/misreads, **Gray.EXE** stays outside the whole system as a fear-driven destroyer who attacks first because he expects harm. (Note: Toby's first email also mentioned a self-harm ending detail; per the same call ChatGPT made in his own thread, that part is not expanded or built into the game — only the carrier/fusion/threat-style mechanics above are.) Added as a **fortieth beat, SIMON CARRIES CLASSICS** (Simon-yellow `#ffd24a` with Classics-violet `#b06bff` accents), on the end of the UNDEFINED LOOP cutscene, right after CLASSICS — THE INFECTION. ## 2026-07-03 — CLASSICS — THE INFECTION: Classics now spreads through beings like cross-pollination — she got inside ToddLLM AND Gray.EXE, and the cross produced ToddLLM 002 as an infected hybrid-form; she keeps the same appearance at any size or spread (a fixed source-organism), turns crazy numbers of the cast into infected or .EXE, and Simon.Exe is the one being immune, standing outside the whole chain (Lore 38 follow-up, "Re: Lore 38 - Endless Staircase has an end, 67 Pirate's Secrets, and more.")

Based on Toby's July 3 email. This message reframes Classics from a one-at-a-time corruptor into a **spread system**. In Toby's words: *"Gray.EXE's ToddLLM 002 form is infected because Classics gotten inside of ToddLLM and Gray.EXE, then came ToddLLM 002 as Gray's new form, just like cross-pollenation. Classics infects each, it can be any size, but always has the same appearence, it can bring the Cross AU or corruption or infection. Simon.Exe is the most powerful being and is immune to Classics' new spreading power. Simon.Exe is a being that can control death itself. ToddLLM 002 is infected and attacks all other characters. Classics makes more and more characters into either infected or .EXE. It is crazy numbers."* So this is the mechanism **behind** the ToddLLM 002 beat: 002 is not a clean evolution but a **hybrid infection-form**, born from Classics crossing into both ToddLLM and Gray at once. Two rules make Classics scarier here. First, she **always keeps the same appearance** no matter her size, spread, infection reach, or AU shift — she is not a shapeshifter but a **fixed source-organism**, visually constant yet functionally invasive, a game-plague core. Second, from that single source she spreads three ways — **Cross AU · corruption · infection** — to **crazy numbers** of characters, turning the whole cast into a **population-level** sort: infected, .EXE, immune, or already gone. And the standout is who is left **out** of the chain: **Simon.Exe is immune** to Classics' new spreading power — the most powerful being, still acting freely while everyone else converts, still able to control death itself. Added as a thirty-ninth beat, **CLASSICS — THE INFECTION** (infection violet `#c24bff` with spore-green `#8bff5a` accents), on the end of the UNDEFINED LOOP cutscene, right after ToddLLM 002 · THE BLAME ENDING. Additive — every earlier beat is untouched.
